  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_709bb3ab-7955-43a7-84f0-0c9e6e549084'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer6943865633199104336"><b>When life crashes down around us, how hard are we willing to fight for the one thing we can’t live without, each other?</b><br/><br/>Life is full of moments. <br/>Big moments. <br/>Little moments. <br/><i>And none of them are inconsequential. </i><br/>Every single moment prepares you for that one instance that defines your life. You must overcome all your fears, confront the demons that chase you, and cleanse the</span>
  <span id="freeText6943865633199104336" style="display:none"><b>When life crashes down around us, how hard are we willing to fight for the one thing we can’t live without, each other?</b><br /><br />Life is full of moments. <br />Big moments. <br />Little moments. <br /><i>And none of them are inconsequential. </i><br />Every single moment prepares you for that one instance that defines your life. You must overcome all your fears, confront the demons that chase you, and cleanse the poison that clings to your soul or you risk the chance of losing everything.<br /><br /><i>Mine started the minute Rylee fell out of that damn storage closet. She made me feel. Made me whole when all I thought I could ever be was incomplete. </i>Became the lifeline I never knew I needed. <i>Hell yes, she’s worth the fight…but how do you fight for someone you know you don’t deserve?</i><br /><br />Love is full of ups and downs. <br />Heart stopping highs.<br />Soul shattering lows.<br /><i>And none of them are insignificant. <i><br />Love is a racecourse of unexpected twists and turns that must be negotiated. You have to break down walls, learn to trust, and heal from your past in order to win. But sometimes it’s the expected that’s the hardest to hold on to.<br /><br /><i>Colton has healed and completed me, stolen my heart, and made me realize our love’s not predictable nor perfect—it’s bent. </i>And bent’s okay. <i>But when outside factors put our relationship to the test, what lengths will I have to go to prove to him that he’s worth the fight?</i><br /><br />Whoever said love is patient and love is kind, never met the two of us. We know our love is worth it—have acknowledged that we were meant to be—but when our pasts crash into our future, will the repercussions make us stronger or break us apart?</i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6943865633199104336" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div id="review_861409671" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/861409671" />
    <a title="K. Bromberg" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1723129-k-bromberg"><img alt="K. Bromberg" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487968849p2/1723129.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/861409671?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K. Bromberg" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K. Bromberg" href="/user/show/1723129-k-bromberg">K. Bromberg</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer861409671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11694443965484244697">Well, what can I say but this is the conclusion to Rylee and Colton's story. It has highs, it has lows, it has healing and angst. If you thought Driven and Fueled took you on an emotional ride, then hold tight, because it's just getting started from page 1 of Crashed on. <br/><br/>Colton's reveal of his past is raw and gritty and not sugar coated...but that also means it's 'real' and you as the reader are in the passenger seat beside him through it all. Rylee deals with a lot too in this book and you root</span>
  <span id="freeText11694443965484244697" style="display:none">Well, what can I say but this is the conclusion to Rylee and Colton's story. It has highs, it has lows, it has healing and angst. If you thought Driven and Fueled took you on an emotional ride, then hold tight, because it's just getting started from page 1 of Crashed on. <br /><br />Colton's reveal of his past is raw and gritty and not sugar coated...but that also means it's 'real' and you as the reader are in the passenger seat beside him through it all. Rylee deals with a lot too in this book and you root for her and Colton each and every step of the way...but you know me, I'm not too predictable, so you'll just have to read to find out what those moments are.<br /><br />I've always said that their love is real...it's not perfect and far from hearts and flowers...but it's theirs. And sometimes when you have to fight hard for someone, you realize just how important they are, how special your bond together is, and you realize that the outside world can fall apart around you, but you'll be okay as long as you have each other. That is Rylee and Colton to me.<br /><br />I hope when you finish reading, that is who they are to you as well.<br /><br />K. Bromberg</span>
  <a data-text-id="11694443965484244697" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_864080791" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/864080791" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/864080791?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer864080791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10752075490550880989"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394052145i/8801522._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%"' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393267486i/8684838._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>^^ this reminds me of Colton & Rylee... :) </i><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br/><br/><strong>A perfect ending to a fantastic series!! </strong><br/><br/><em>Crashed</em> was an intense, emotional, riveting ride from A to motherf*cking Z. It's a story that makes you believe in the resilience and healing power of love. Colton and Rylee's journey is sexy, romantic, heart breaking and uplifting. This is the kind of book you don't want to put down and you can't wait to read more of, and without a doubt, the Driven Trilogy will forever be one of my</span>
  <span id="freeText10752075490550880989" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394052145i/8801522._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width='100%"' src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393267486i/8684838._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>^^ this reminds me of Colton &amp; Rylee... :) </i><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br><br><strong>A perfect ending to a fantastic series!! </strong><br><br><em>Crashed</em> was an intense, emotional, riveting ride from A to motherf*cking Z. It's a story that makes you believe in the resilience and healing power of love. Colton and Rylee's journey is sexy, romantic, heart breaking and uplifting. This is the kind of book you don't want to put down and you can't wait to read more of, and without a doubt, the Driven Trilogy will forever be one of my top favorites!!<br><br>This book started off right where the last one ended -- the moment after that heart stopping cliffhanger -- with an absolutely <em>amazing</em> prologue that brought tears to my eyes and sent chills through my body. It was easily one of the best prologues I've read and from the first line, I was transported right back into the story.<br><br>The emotions hit strong right from the start -- the desperation of the situation, the vivid imagery, the <em>writing... </em>it was so well put together. I have quotes highlighted everywhere throughout my book.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>Devastation surrenders, desperation consumes, life splutters, and yet my soul clings.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>Superman.</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Gosh, even thinking of Colton's beloved superheroes makes me choked up!! <em>"A childhood obsession now turned into an adult's grasp on hope."</em> -- They were such a fantastic addition to the whole series. The way these 4 names -- <em>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</em><strong>
  <em> -- </em>
</strong>were woven into the story was so subtle but yet so powerful that each time I read one of their names, my heart squeezed.<br><br>I don't want to say much about the plot at all because this is the final book in the series and, as a direct continuation of the story, it should not be read on it's own... and if you <em>have </em>read the other books, then I don't want to give anything away so I'll just tell you how this book made me feel instead.<br><br>One of the many highlights of this book for me was that it took the time to highlight these incredibly emotionally meaningful 'bonding' scenes between the main characters -- Colton's Dad and Rylee ("<em>The first time I saw him, he broke my heart and stole it all with one, single look."</em>), Colton and his Dad, Colton and the kids at The House (<em>"The damaged man helping the broken child</em>"), Colton and Rylee's Dad ("<em>The unspoken bond from father to the man his daughter loves passes between them. Man to man. Protector to protector."</em>). And of course, the central relationship in this story: Colton and Rylee...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"<em>I swear to God she's the only air my body can breathe. Fuck if she's not everything I need and nothing I deserve."</em>
</blockquote>
</b><br>I loved the way Colton and Ryle were together. Yin and yang in so many ways despite their differences. Rylee was just so perceptive, and so understanding, and holy shit did she ever have a badass side too. Ok -- I <em>love</em> it when the guys get all growly and protective of their women but there was this scene where Rylee stood up for Colton that was just pure fucking awesome!! And <em>then</em> seeing Colton stand up for her in return.... ohhhh my heart was singing!! It was just one of the <em>many</em> epic moments in this series.<br><br>I absolutely adore tortured Alpha male heroes -- without a doubt, they are my favorite -- and Colton Donavan was the embodiment of the kind of hero I most easily fall for. I felt <em>so </em>heart broken for the things that happened to him in his past, and for the emotionally crippling scars they'd left on him. His struggle to face the nightmares his past felt so real because with the way it was written, and the glimpses at his POV too, you really <em>felt </em>how hard it was for him. I just loved watching the progression of his healing throughout the series. Knowing how strong and deeply rooted his pain was gave so much more meaning to each little victory step forward and to each little bit of healing.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"I want to be your motherfucking checkered flag, Rylee. Your pace car to lead you through tough times, your pit stop when you need a break, your start line, your finish line, your goddamn victory lane."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I've said this before and I'll say it again, Rylee was just a fantastic heroine. I absolutely <em>loved</em> how she could always see right through Colton and always knew where he was at, even when he couldn't find it in him to admit or say it, even when he was being a total ass, she just saw right through it. It might sound weird to say this but it was just genuinely refreshing to have a heroine who didn't make stupid decisions. One who was smart, capable, and independent while also being totally in love with her guy.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I hold tight letting him know that no matter how far he falls, I'll catch him. I'll always catch him."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Now, part way through there was a development in the story that put my heart in my throat because I was <em>so </em>worried at the direction it would take the story in. It opened the doors for all kinds of frustrating drama but I just want to say how <em>thrilled</em> I was to see that once again, even though it was an intense, angst-ridden issue, and while Colton and Ryle may have stumbled a bit while dealing with it, instead of being broken down, they allowed it make them stronger than ever before. I was honestly just proud of them.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We can do this… It's just this selfless girl and this healing boy and we can really make this work."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The way each issue in this book was dealt with, worked through and overcome was just so emotionally captivating and heart felt. And I especially <em>loved</em> how, throughout the course of the series, there was a whole list of words and phases that grew to have <em>so </em> much meaning and memories behind them -- the superheroes, 'racing', 747, cotton candy, pit stops, text songs, the motherfucking checkered flag, the alphabet A--Z, sheets, the lifeline... and so many more little things like that.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"God, I fucking race you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And lets not forget the scorching hot steam factor here. Seriously -- these books are HOT HOT HOTTTT!!! Colton and Rylee had an intense chemistry that left me fanning myself over and over again. Sex was an important part of their connection and healing, but I loved the way the love scenes never overshadowed the general plotline but rather complimented it. This is Adult romance done <em>right </em>with a wonderful balance between sex and emotional character growth.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want every inch of you trembling, fucking shaking, begging me to take you, Ry, because fuck if I won't be doing the same. I want to be your sigh, your moan, your cry out in pleasure and every fucking sound in between."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ohhhh, and the ending was just perfect!! I'm not going to spoil it for you but I'll just say that I loved the way everything came together and definitely shed a few happy tears. Colton and Rylee had just come so far over the course of this series. They deserved every bit of happiness that they got.<br><br>And -- two words: Double. Epilogue. :D<br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5+ stars</strong><br><br>PS - I'm so excited that we're going to be getting a book about Becks and Haddie next!!! They were both witty, charming, fun and wise... just all-round fantastic characters who I can't wait to see in the spotlight!!!<br><br><b>MY REVIEW of BOOK #1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1dgJMql">http://bit.ly/1dgJMql</a> <br>MY REVIEW of BOOK #2: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1hOO53F">http://bit.ly/1hOO53F</a><br><br>****************************<br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10752075490550880989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_617951843" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617951843" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617951843?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617951843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9029401851384781465"><b>5 is simply not enough stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795799._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>**Note, minor spoilers for those who have not read the first two books.**<br/><br/>We begin Crashed right were Fueled left off. A fireball of destruction that left our mouths gaping open, our pulse racing and tears in our eyes. Hearts around the world faltered in that moment. <br/><br/>As the smoke clears and the medical staff rushes in, Colton has a moment. A pure and beautiful moment that holds such a deeper meaning than I ever imagined it would. But that is not the end of the pain we</span>
  <span id="freeText9029401851384781465" style="display:none"><b>5 is simply not enough stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795799._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**Note, minor spoilers for those who have not read the first two books.**<br><br>We begin Crashed right were Fueled left off. A fireball of destruction that left our mouths gaping open, our pulse racing and tears in our eyes. Hearts around the world faltered in that moment. <br><br>As the smoke clears and the medical staff rushes in, Colton has a moment. A pure and beautiful moment that holds such a deeper meaning than I ever imagined it would. But that is not the end of the pain we must suffer through. He has to recover, he has to survive. <br><br>Rylee is facing her worst fear, reliving a nightmare she barely escaped from the first time. As she waits for Colton to return to her, to remember the words that he spoke to her moments before the crash, her world stops.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795800.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>We’ve had two books to get to know these two and to fall utterly in love with them. Where Driven gave us such a perfect glimpse into who Rylee was, Fueled gave us Colton and all his broken glory. Crashed felt more like it was Colton’s story for the most part, since there was so much he still had to let go of, although it blended perfectly into their story in the end.<br><br>There are so many moments in this book that ensured that I was an emotional disaster, for every fractured part of my heart that was healed, there was a new crack forming. It was two steps forward and one step back for about 60% of this book. An utterly fantastic symphony of highs and lows that ensured that every moment was felt deep into your bones. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795801.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can’t say much more about this journey without spoiling the really fantastic moments or the really crappy ones (let’s just say Tawny stars in most of those moments), so I will let you discover these on your own. What I will say is that my hat is off to Kristy Bromberg. With the first two books being so successful, Crashed had a lot to live up to and she pulled it off. By far this was my favorite of the series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795802.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Colton was the perfect broken bad boy that you can’t help but love. But he wasn’t just a little broken, he was shattered completely. There was barely dust when he completely broke, it was beautiful and heartbreaking all at the same time. <br><br>I love the fact that although when I first read Driven a few of the corny racing one-liners that they shared made me roll my eyes, now after finishing Crashed; those same lines had me smiling like a loon. That is something that you can only accomplish when you can get your readers to connect to the characters, and there is not one piece of this entire cast (with the exception of Tawny) that I did not love.<br><br>Becks was always there to push Colton when he needed it and was so supportive of Rylee. Haddie kept you entertained with her off the wall comments.<br><br><i>
  <b> “Shit, the only reason to kick a man like him out of bed would be to fuck him on the floor.”</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394007718i/8795803.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had a smile on my face for the last 30% of this story that was so big that my face hurt. And not only do we get a fantastic epilogue, we get a bonus one that was just icing on the cake and brought us back to the very start of this story in so many ways. <br><br>This series started off with such a bang and had the great bad boy – good girl romance, but where K took us in this veered completely off the path and gave us so much more in the end. I cannot wait for Beck &amp; Had’s story but I am nowhere near ready to let these two go. <br><br>Kristy Bromberg has wowed me as a reader with her talent through her words and has impressed me as person by her grace. I implore you to read this series if you have not yet, it is 100% worth it. <br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>=============================<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421956ra/838929.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421957ra/838930.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9029401851384781465" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_723969187" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/723969187" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9532349-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/723969187?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/9532349-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=swoon-worthy-men">swoon-worthy-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=gut-wrenching-heart-melting">gut-wrenching-heart-melting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=bad-boy-alpha-male">bad-boy-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9532349-caitlin?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer723969187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11908903394961336464"><b>5 “A to Z” Stars!!<br/><br/>When I first picked this series up, it was just another book to read. But after that first book, I knew it meant so much more. Rylee and Colton have found a special place in my heart and K. Bromberg gave them the most epically fantastic, healing, loving, perfect ending that exceeded all my expectations.</b><br/><br/><b>Rylee</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383353314i/6518062._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Colton</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437259i/884295._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='520' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Any doubts I had about Rylee and Colton (and there weren’t many) were completely assuaged in <i>Crashed </i>and even though they still had their fair share of up and downs, t</span>
  <span id="freeText11908903394961336464" style="display:none"><b>5 “A to Z” Stars!!<br><br>When I first picked this series up, it was just another book to read. But after that first book, I knew it meant so much more. Rylee and Colton have found a special place in my heart and K. Bromberg gave them the most epically fantastic, healing, loving, perfect ending that exceeded all my expectations.</b><br><br><b>Rylee</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383353314i/6518062._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Colton</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437259i/884295._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="520" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Any doubts I had about Rylee and Colton (and there weren’t many) were completely assuaged in <i>Crashed </i>and even though they still had their fair share of up and downs, they found their happy ending. If you’ve read the first two books in this series, then you have to read this one. And if you haven’t picked this series up yet, what are you waiting for?? This series has gotten better and better with every book, culminating in this wonderful ending to Colton and Rylee’s story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“This is love. Me and him, making it work. One being strong when the other is weak. Thinking of the other first when they know their partner is going to feel pain.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I’m not going to talk about the plot because everything means more if you don’t know about it ahead of time. So I’ll start with the best and my personal favorite part of this book. Mr. Colton Donovan!! Omg this man has completely stolen my heart. From the first moment, even when he was a cocky asshole, I couldn’t help but fall for him. The emotional journey he goes on in this one is truly inspiring and I can’t even imagine surviving what he went through. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I try to cover my ears like a fucking little kid because it’s too much. All of it—the words, the fear, the fucking hope that I just might in fact be a little bent and not completely broken—is just too much.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>His story completely broke my heart, shattered it into a million pieces. Colton had to dig deep in this one and finally face the past he’s been running from for so long. And the prologue was both heartbreaking and chilling at the same time. Underneath his tough exterior, is this broken man who doesn’t know how to be loved. But he’s still extremely sweet, protective, caring, and just all around the best guy. I loved seeing him with Rylee and the boys at the house. He has a huge heart even if he might not realize it. For so long, he thought if anyone found out his past, they would reject him and it was beautiful to see him open himself up to others and find acceptance and love for the first time.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I want to be your motherfucking checkered flag, Rylee. Your pace car to lead you through tough times, your pit stop when you need a break, your start line, your finish line, your goddam victory lane.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Okay, I think that’s enough Colton ranting for now...Onto Rylee. She’s one of my favorite females because she’s strong, deeply protective, caring, loving and stood by Colton through everything. Rylee has her own heartbreaking past and I don’t even know how she not only picked herself back up but learned to thrive in her environment. She’s extremely nurturing with the boys and Colton but I loved that she was also willing to give Colton his space when he needed it. <br><br>Rylee is also so understanding of everyone. Even when Colton would try to push her away or lash out at her, she saw deep down into his soul how much he was really hurting. She didn’t run or avoid but gave Colton enough room to breathe and come to terms with whatever they were facing. She showed Colton unwavering unconditional love and that he wasn’t alone in his pain. Rylee was there for him no matter what.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I want him to know that his pain is my pain. His shame is my shame. His adversity is my adversity. His struggle is my struggle. That he no longer has to battle it along, body and soul stained in silent shame.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>They both faced some really tough times in this book but it just made them that much stronger. Colton and Rylee have had that spark between them from the very beginning but they have not had an easy road whatsoever. All they’ve had to go through, all the fights and breakups, and misunderstandings were all worth it in the end. And I think all their experiences showed each of them just how strong they could be.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Because we need to crack. We need to break. Only then can we pick up each other’s pieces and make each other whole again.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved that throughout this series, there have been so many little things that signify so much between Colton and Rylee. <i>Ace, a motherfucking checkered flag, sheets, the alphabet, racing, non-negotiables, 4 super heroes, song texts, a storage closet.</i> Every moment between them was something to cherish and have helped to shape them into who they are now. They’ve grown together, learned how to be together, and while their love isn’t perfect, it’s real.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m not expecting anything anymore because if being with Colton has taught me anything, it’s that our love isn’t patient, nor is it kind, it’s just uniquely ours.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The sex scenes were h-o-t hot but its so much more than just sex between Colton and Rylee now. There weren’t as many smexy times as in the previous books but I was totally okay with that because this story was about so much more.<br><br>Oh and breakout star of this book is definitely Becks. We saw a little of him in Fueled but oh my gosh, I completely fell for him in this one. I love the friendship he has with Colton even when all they do is egg each other on. Becks wasn’t afraid to give Colton the hard truths and make Colton face his fears. And he was always there for Rylee too. Supporting her, reminding her how much she meant to Colton when she may have had doubts. I hope he gets his own story one day! Here is just one of the many hilarious moments between Becks and Colton:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You—Colton Donovan—stepped foot into a grocery store?”<br>“Yep.”<br>“And it wasn’t just to buy condoms?”<br>I can’t help it now. I love fucking with him. It’s just too goddamn easy.<br>“Nah, no longer a requirement when you hold a frequent flier card to the barebacking club.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don’t think it hit me until the end that this was really the end of Colton and Rylee’s story, and when it did, it hit me hard. I’ve been right there in this story with them, felt every emotion that passed between them, experienced all the highs and lows, which makes saying goodbye that much harder. K has so much talent in her writing and storytelling and she truly brought everything to a close in this book. Nothing felt rushed or forced and I loved every second of it. She’s also so unconventional, whenever I thought I knew where the story was going, there’d be a twist that completely changed the direction of it.<br><br>The ending seriously put this hugest grin on my face. At the gym reading the last 100 pages or so, just on the elliptical grinning like a weirdo. Then lying in bed reading the double epilogue, yup DOUBLE EPILOGUE, I had a smile on my face. The ending was absolute perfection and everything I could have wished for for Colton and Rylee. It made saying bye to them that much harder but lessened the blow at the same time. Some of the lines were so beautiful, they made my heart ache with joy. To see how far, Rylee and Colton have both come on their journey warmed my soul and showed me again exactly why this series is one of my favorites.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“You were the one thing I never wanted—never, ever expected in my life—an fuck if I can live without you now. You test me and tempt me and make me look at the truth I don’t want to face and are stubborn as hell, but God, baby, I wouldn’t want you any other way. Wouldn’t want us any other way.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I think I have the most quotes from any book I’ve ever read and I wish I could share all of them. But really, just read this book! It was amazing and perfect and I wish I would read it for the first time again. I’ve been waiting for this book since I finished the second one and I was not disappointed! Colton and Rylee are one of my favorite book couples and I will not be able to let them go for a long time. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I want to be your first, your last, and every fucking thing in between.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><b><u>UPDATE 1.29.2014</u><br>OMG there's a cover!!! And I love it :D </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391032875i/8320122._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>When life crashes down around us, how hard are we willing to fight for the one thing we can’t live without, each other?<br><br>Life is full of moments. <br>Big moments. <br>Little moments. <br>And none of them are inconsequential. <br>Every single moment prepares you for that one instance that defines your life. You must overcome all your fears, confront the demons that chase you, and cleanse the poison that clings to your soul or you risk the chance of losing everything.<br><br>Mine started the minute Rylee fell out of that damn storage closet. She made me feel. Made me whole when all I thought I could ever be was incomplete. Became the lifeline I never knew I needed. Hell yes, she’s worth the fight…but how do you fight for someone you know you don’t deserve?<br><br>Love is full of ups and downs. <br>Heart stopping highs.<br>Soul shattering lows.<br>And none of them are insignificant. <br>Love is a racecourse of unexpected twists and turns that must be negotiated. You have to break down walls, learn to trust, and heal from your past in order to win. But sometimes it’s the expected that’s the hardest to hold on to.<br><br>Colton has healed and completed me, stolen my heart, and made me realize our love’s not predictable nor perfect—it’s bent. And bent’s okay. But when outside factors put our relationship to the test, what lengths will I have to go to prove to him that he’s worth the fight?<br><br>Whoever said love is patient and love is kind, never met the two of us. We know our love is worth it—have acknowledged that we were meant to be—but when our pasts crash into our future, will the repercussions make us stronger or break us apart?</i><br><br><br><b>Just finished the second book with that devastating cliffhanger. Need this book <u>now</u>!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11908903394961336464" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1141177760" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1141177760" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1141177760?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer7794213135199006914"> <b>5 Crashing Stars.</b><br/>	<br/>This third book starts after the dreadful end of the second. And after the worst has passed, a lot more is yet to come. Without fully memory of the last days, some people will try to take advantage of Colton, creating again, more drama and more fight between him and Rylee.   <span id="freeText7794213135199006914" style="display:none"> <b>5 Crashing Stars.</b><br>	<br>This third book starts after the dreadful end of the second. And after the worst has passed, a lot more is yet to come. Without fully memory of the last days, some people will try to take advantage of Colton, creating again, more drama and more fight between him and Rylee. And Rylee is tired of fighting against everyone and everything for Colton, especially against Colton himself. <br>But Colton knows that this time is all or nothing, he’s decided to fight his demons and give Rylee what she deserves. And now he finds himself in the race of his life, with Rylee waiting on the victory lane, but his ghosts still trapping on the starting line. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419622508i/13099405._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If the first two books almost gave me a heart attack, this one redeemed everything. What an amazing end for an amazing series. In the beginning we still had some angsts and a lot of angst, but when everything started falling in place, it was like a prolonged epilogue and I loved every second of it. <br>Definitely, my favorite book of the series, and a greatly written end. If you want a steamy and romantic story, with enough drama to keep you entertained, these books are a great choice. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> I already was a Rylee fan in the previous books, so liking her in this one wasn’t a surprise. I ended this book hoping for a story between Haddie and Beck, and since I’ve found out that it will be one, I have nothing more to ask for! <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Abuse, abortion…  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <div id="review_857105645" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/857105645" />
    <a title="Kimberly " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11898871-kimberly"><img alt="Kimberly " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474058001p2/11898871.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/857105645?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kimberly " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kimberly " href="/user/show/11898871-kimberly">Kimberly </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11898871-kimberly?shelf=loved">loved</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer857105645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5292909081967262126"><b>
  <i>“I’m driven by fear…Fueled with desperation…crashing into the unknown.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>PERFECTION. Sweet baby Jesus, K. Bromberg has won herself a motherfu**ing checkered flag with this book. This book is the much-anticipated final book in the Driven Trilogy and it did not disappoint. Instead, it exceeded every expectation I ever had and I am left sitting here writing this review feeling a complete state of euphoric book hangover bliss.<br/><br/>In short, this book had one of the BEST ENDINGS I have ever read thus fa</span>
  <span id="freeText5292909081967262126" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“I’m driven by fear…Fueled with desperation…crashing into the unknown.”</i>
</b><br /><br />PERFECTION. Sweet baby Jesus, K. Bromberg has won herself a motherfu**ing checkered flag with this book. This book is the much-anticipated final book in the Driven Trilogy and it did not disappoint. Instead, it exceeded every expectation I ever had and I am left sitting here writing this review feeling a complete state of euphoric book hangover bliss.<br /><br />In short, this book had one of the BEST ENDINGS I have ever read thus far. Kristy was able to give Colton &amp; Rylee such a complete and perfect ending, that quite frankly, I am in awe of her. It is painfully obvious how much this author has lived, breathed, slept Colton &amp; Rylee – so much that she knew that this was the ending they would need, that I would need, that you would need. Every question was answered. Every issue addressed. I felt so satisfied with this story that there was nothing I would change about it.<br /><br />Be prepared to feel every emotion possible while reading. Have some Kleenex, a bottle of vodka (or tequila if that’s how you roll), remove all breakables, and throw in some chocolate while you are at it. You will laugh, you will swoon, you will get hot &amp; bothered, you will cry, you will scream WTF multiple times, you will want to hug K. Bromberg and then you will want to strangle her. It was written in a way that has the reader so emotionally connected and involved with both Colton &amp; Rylee that what they felt, you felt. I feel like I ran a marathon and I am completely emotionally spent – in the best possible way!<br /><br />I’m sure you are sitting there questioning how authentic this review is. I’m gushing. I never gush. I know that and you probably know that too. But, there are times where you read a series that just affects you in a certain way that you just have to gush about. This is one of those series for me. I love series with hot, Alpha men, tons of angst and a story that will touch my soul. There are tons out there, I know. So what makes this one so amazing you ask? Let me make a list:<br /><br />Colton’s Dark Past. I, like everyone else, love a tortured hero. I love a tough Alpha male who is wounded and needs saving. And Colton’s past is dark, yet heartbreaking. If you’ve read FUELED, you know what lies in his past and you know what plagues his thoughts. My heart broke for him. This book really focused on Colton dealing with his past, instead of burying it with booze, women and racing. It was so gut wrenching at times that I shed tear after tear for him. I love how Kristy handled his story arc – how she really had Colton face his demons. It would’ve been very easy for her to just loosely touch on his past, but she chose a different route. A route that included digging deep and opening himself up for the first time. I was so proud of him for how far he has come and I love him a little bit more because of it.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“My heart pounds and my head knows she just might have scaled that final fucking steel wall, opened it up like fucking Pandora’s box so all the evil locked forever within could take flight and exit my soul with just one thing left remaining. Fucking hope.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Unexpected Story Lines and Plot. This book started full steam ahead. Kristy didn’t ease us back into the story, rather she hit the ground running. At about 10% I remember my heart beating so fast and my emotions being all over the place. This may be a final book, but let me be clear A LOT OF THINGS HAPPEN – unexpected things that you did not see coming. I was on the edge of my seat and each time a new conflict or plot twist happened I became that much more addicted to this story. Read below for my status updates while reading!<br /><br />Character Growth. Oh my have these two characters come a long way. I remember in the first book, Colton was always so hot and cold with Rylee. He pushed her away when she got too close, but then after being apart, he drew her back in. And Rylee was no different. She craved him, but then ran away when things got too hard. It was exhausting keeping up with them. But over the last two books, I actually saw the growth in both characters. If I was questioning (which I wasn’t, but if I was) whether Colton &amp; Rylee belonged together, all doubt was removed in this book. These characters have balls of steel when it comes to each other and it was such a pleasure to watch them actually realize that they needed each other like they needed air to breathe. No they weren’t perfect and yes there were times where they almost regressed to their old ways, but it is very obvious how much they’ve grown together.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This is love. Me and him, making it work. One being strong when the other is weak. Thinking of the other first when they know their partner is going to feel pain.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Sexy Time. I cannot write this review without talking about the steam factor that this book has. *Fans self* Colton is the epitome of what most woman (okay maybe it’s just me) desires in the bedroom. The sex scenes were not just sex – they had emotion, passion, depth to them. You felt the sexual chemistry between Colton and Rylee more so than in the other two books because quite frankly, they race each other. It’s more than sex with them.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I want every inch of you trembling, fucking shaking, begging for me to take you, Ry, because fuck if I won’t be doing the same. I want to be your sigh, your moan, your cry out in pleasure and every fucking sound in between.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Colton’s Smart Mouth. Geez sometimes I wanted to smack him upside the head followed by pulling him to me to make out with him. He’s one of THOSE guys. The kind that gets under your skin and lives up to Rylee’s A.C.E nickname, while at the same time makes you want him even more.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“A man has to have his priorities.” He smirks. “If one head’s fucked up, at least the other one can be used to its maximum potential.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Perfect Ending. The ending was by far my favorite part of the book for me. I absolutely adored how Kristy handled the ending to Colton &amp; Rylee’s story. I’m going to gush – this was one of the best endings I have ever read in any book. It was the perfect way to wrap up the entire series and I couldn’t ask for anything better. If you are a fan of Colton &amp; Rylee, then I know, without a shadow of a doubt, that you will LOVE this ending as much as I did. Your heart will swell with love and pride for these two characters. I am still reeling from reading it and I know it will stay with me always.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I want to be your motherfucking checkered flag, Rylee. Your pace car to lead you through tough times, your pit stop when you need a break, your start line, your finish line, your goddamn victory line.”</i>
</b><br /><br />As a side note, I need to mention that as much as I loved Rylee &amp; Colton, I am also so in love with Haddie and Becks. OMG these two characters are hilarious and I am so addicted to them. They are probably the best secondary characters/best friends and I am so glad they will be getting their own book in the near future. I love their quick wit and snarky comebacks and know that their story will be one hell of a ride.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Yours is damn hard not to talk about when he looks like that with his sexy swagger, come-fuck-me eyes, and all around holy hotness. Shit, the only reason to kick a man like him out of bed would be to fuck him on the floor.” – Haddie</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You don’t get it, do you? Fuck the A or the B, you have the whole goddamn alphabet upstairs and she’s asleep in your fucking bed right now, but the only letter that can fuck this up is U.” – Becks</i>
</b><br /><br />Believe all the hype. THIS BOOK ROCKS! It has cemented the Driven Trilogy as one of my favorite series and I cannot wait for each and every one of you to read this. Despite what you may have heard or what you think, know this – K. Bromberg has created a story and characters that will stay with you forever. I will forever think of Colton Donovan whenever I see a race car, checkered flag or cotton candy &lt;3<br /><br /><i>*ARC received from author in exchange for an honest review*</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15448153036605946512"><b>5 (+) NEVER inconsequential stars</b><br/><br/><b>“Remember, life isn’t about how you survive the storm, but rather how you dance in the rain.”</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986110i/8792203.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>For Colton Donavan and Rylee Thomas...the journey through the storm of their lives was brutal, it was sexy, and most of all it was beautiful when that "checkered flag" was finally taken forever.<br/><br/>After the "Crash"...life stopped...then it began slowly, cautiously and with pit stops all around. Never have two characters fought themselves or the elements to make it. K Bromber</span>
  <span id="freeText15448153036605946512" style="display:none"><b>5 (+) NEVER inconsequential stars</b><br><br><b>“Remember, life isn’t about how you survive the storm, but rather how you dance in the rain.”</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986110i/8792203.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>For Colton Donavan and Rylee Thomas...the journey through the storm of their lives was brutal, it was sexy, and most of all it was beautiful when that "checkered flag" was finally taken forever.<br><br>After the "Crash"...life stopped...then it began slowly, cautiously and with pit stops all around. Never have two characters fought themselves or the elements to make it. K Bromberg has catapulted this series to the top of my list...From broken bones to a soul that was shattered, Colton's character was existing in his world of arrangements, but just one crashing moment....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986229i/8792223.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Rylee Thomas got to Colton like no other!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986110i/8792204.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>“I love who you are and what you make me. I love that your spark has stopped the blur. That you wanted to race with me. That I don't need the superheroes anymore because I need you instead."</b><br><br>Finally Colton understands the chaos inside his heart. He faces his past and he finds everything he never knew he wanted or needed. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986424i/8792241._SY540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes He RACES Rylee...as he truly LOVES her he finally understands it...which is truly a great thing since now it is time for Rylee to need him like never before. Are they worth it? is what they have real? or is it just between the sheets?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393986110ra/8792205.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"Relationships aren’t easy. They’re hard and can be brutal at times … but those are the times you learn the most about yourself."</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393986110i/8792206.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Colton Donavan has captivated me and he now owns me completely. This read was full of quotable sections that I want to re-read forever. I loved the passionate intimacy and the raw lust that Colton and Rylee had for one another. Not only were they intense, but reading their scenes felt like breathing them in. I am a believer in Happy ever after, but never when it occurs without struggle! Thank you to this author for this conclusion and the caution laps that kept the race off pace...for me...CRASHED was everthing...A to F'ng Z!!!!</span>

Rylee realizes just how important Colton is to her, and that he is her everything.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/0b7078db-228d-42ea-a2d0-6536d475fdc7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I loved the sexy, cocky Colton, and his sweet Ryles! I still couldn't stand nasty ass ho Tawny, but adored all of Rylee's boys &amp; her best friend Haddie. Can't wait for Haddie &amp; Becks book! :D<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a42314e3-7bd6-45ac-a69a-514607777aa8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>-Rylee. I need to see her. Don't want to be alone anymore. I need to feel her. Don't want to be broken anymore.<br><br>-Call me a pussy, but I swear to God she's the only air my body can breathe. Fuck if she's not everything I need and nothing that I deserve.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/baff41a4-3057-45b7-b832-df5d44d56f2e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>-"What's best for me? Don't you know what's best for me is you, Colton? Every single part of you. The stubborn, the wild and reckless, the fun loving, the serious, and even the broken parts of you," I tell him, pressing my lips to his between every word. Only you."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/667fcf07-03b5-4981-b995-85fb6ec63c3f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I really, really race you."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/94c2e2e9-3919-472f-88ca-30bbed7dafeb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

He sighs "...it's as fucking real as real can get.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/17b81d69-2d42-4233-85ad-b96b77d00165.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

My eyes flutter open and look up to lose myself in the beauty of his face. "I want to watch you as I take you. I want to watch you as you let me love you."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/cd57fffa-565c-4288-99b6-362a3e4494b9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394811407i/8909616.jpg" alt=" photo cd57fffa-565c-4288-99b6-362a3e4494b9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-My breath catches in my throat as I come to the realization that I want this. I fucking want her. In my life- day, night, now, later- and the thought staggers me. Breaks and mends me. Tames the un-fucking-tamable. Fuckin'A. I shake my head and laugh softly. I guess I should say A to fucking Z.<br><br>-You were the bright spot- that fucking spark- I couldn't hide from even when the darkness claimed me.<br><br>-Motherfucking checkered flags and alphabets and sheets.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/6a26dd62-dce0-43d6-9241-2c76ed0a63cc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394829729i/8912828.jpg" alt=" photo 6a26dd62-dce0-43d6-9241-2c76ed0a63cc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-I feel her hand on my back, feel her lips press against my shoulder, and open my eyes to look at her- my whole fucking alphabet- and smile.<br><br>-"Remember, hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn't it good to be alive?"<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/86c61ae5-2f57-4907-b761-7a98f619fbb2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394029602i/8798124.jpg" alt=" photo 86c61ae5-2f57-4907-b761-7a98f619fbb2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_704475679" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/704475679" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/704475679?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-like-your-tats">i-like-your-tats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=athletes">athletes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=thumbs-up-leading-lady">thumbs-up-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=tickle-my-funny-bone">tickle-my-funny-bone</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704475679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5908492183430907222"><br/><b>***4.5 Checkered Flag Stars***</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”Hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn’t it good to be alive?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386692114ra/7420752.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”Remember, life isn’t about how you survive the storm, but rather how you dance in the rain.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>What a great conclusion to a fantastic series! <br/><br/>Rylee’s strength was the foundation of this book and Colton’s transformation was what romance readers live for. EVERY moment inside his head broke and healed my heart. Watching him struggle with his heart, mind, body and soul was ag</span>
  <span id="freeText5908492183430907222" style="display:none"><br><b>***4.5 Checkered Flag Stars***</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”Hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn’t it good to be alive?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386692114ra/7420752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”Remember, life isn’t about how you survive the storm, but rather how you dance in the rain.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>What a great conclusion to a fantastic series! <br><br>Rylee’s strength was the foundation of this book and Colton’s transformation was what romance readers live for. EVERY moment inside his head broke and healed my heart. Watching him struggle with his heart, mind, body and soul was agonizing, but so worth it. To watch Colton and Rylee explore the depth of their feelings for each other, understand where they belong in each other’s lives and ultimately, witness Colton’s battle, hopeful acceptance and closure to his past...it was heartbreakingly beautiful. With determination, sheer will and unyielding love...they conquered it all. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>His past, his fears, his shame.<br><br>My past, my fears, my grief.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468592692ra/19726088.gif" alt="" height="295" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There’s no way I can accurately review this book without spoiling the first two…so I’m not going to. I will just say that this series is a MUST READ. And I will beg and plead with you not to be discouraged after completing the first book (unless you loved it, then feel free to ignore me!). It was a rough one for me, but I understand now. It was a debut...an author wanting to tell a beautiful love story but unsure of her footing. Well, let me tell you that she found her voice real fast and you really see the growth of an author, as well as the characters, over the course of this series. <br><br>This is definitely a series that will stay in my heart for some time. There are so many sayings and nuances that now any time I hear will instantly transport me back to the emotions I felt while reading this series. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”We can do this… It's just this selfless girl and this healing boy and we can really make this work.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403230340ra/10061681.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5908492183430907222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_673009408" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/673009408" />
    <a title="Cara Arthur" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16904082-cara-arthur"><img alt="Cara Arthur" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433557092p2/16904082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/673009408?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cara Arthur" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cara Arthur" href="/user/show/16904082-cara-arthur">Cara Arthur</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673009408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11021295637228876692">Reviewing on behalf of A Book Whores Obsession:<br/><br/>K. Bromberg faced a near impossible task – write a conclusion that would compare to the brilliance of Driven & Fueled, the best-selling series that drove book fans wild across the world. Well, bring out the checkered flags because, not only did she deliver, she wrote the most epic final installment of a series to date!<br/>Exploding with passion, angst, and drama, Crashed assaults the reader’s every emotion in one delicious novel. Colton and Rylee are ba</span>
  <span id="freeText11021295637228876692" style="display:none">Reviewing on behalf of A Book Whores Obsession:<br /><br />K. Bromberg faced a near impossible task – write a conclusion that would compare to the brilliance of Driven &amp; Fueled, the best-selling series that drove book fans wild across the world. Well, bring out the checkered flags because, not only did she deliver, she wrote the most epic final installment of a series to date!<br />Exploding with passion, angst, and drama, Crashed assaults the reader’s every emotion in one delicious novel. Colton and Rylee are back on the heels of the dramatic conclusion of book two - “Fueled”. Faced with an uncertain future following the ‘rookie’s mistake’ that left the world hanging, Crashed follows the beloved characters as they attempt to go forward, to put the past behind them. Of course, nothing is ever easy with Colton Donavan and K. Bromberg takes our minds, hearts, and wits on a race of a lifetime. <br />This book will pull you from every angle – you will laugh, cry, sob, swoon, and feel like your heart is going to burst. I have never experienced a book that touched me on so many levels; I related to these characters in so many ways - as a friend, a lover, and simply as a human being. I’ve spent a lot of time trying to figure out how K. Bromberg did it – how did she really ‘get’ to me like this? While I may never figure it out exactly, I realize this – she made these characters come alive in a way that rarely happens. Colton, Rylee, and Beckett aren’t just people on paper – I feel like they are my friends. I can hear their voices, I can hear their laughs, and I can see their smiles. I felt their hearts break and I wanted to offer comfort. I saw them happy and my heart swelled. <br />Closing the book doesn’t make the story go away, it simply lives on in your subconscious and in your heart. This is truly one series that you will carry with you forever. Now, while we wait for Becks’ book next, we will do what all book whores do – we re-read the series that crashed its' way into our psyche – the story that was “A to motherfucking Z”. <br />Well done, K. Bromberg. Well done. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11021295637228876692" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_621600538" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/621600538" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/621600538?book_show_action=true">May 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=erotica-romantica-read">erotica-romantica-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=5-star-reads">5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=contemporary-romance-read">contemporary-romance-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=arc-from-author-read">arc-from-author-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer621600538" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer820134051479600082"><br/>"God, I fucking race you," he says to me.<br/><br/><br/>Me to you, K. Bromberg: I fucking race YOU!<br/><br/>Where do I start? Where do I even start?! I've watched this author grow by superhero-sized leaps and bounds over the course of this series. I've witnessed her grab the reigns of her talent and take total, masterful control. Crashed is the culmination of not only Colton and Rylee's journey, but, in a certain way, that of the author's, as well. And both are triumphant!<br/><br/>This series is everything a true fan of romance</span>
  <span id="freeText820134051479600082" style="display:none"><br />"God, I fucking race you," he says to me.<br /><br /><br />Me to you, K. Bromberg: I fucking race YOU!<br /><br />Where do I start? Where do I even start?! I've watched this author grow by superhero-sized leaps and bounds over the course of this series. I've witnessed her grab the reigns of her talent and take total, masterful control. Crashed is the culmination of not only Colton and Rylee's journey, but, in a certain way, that of the author's, as well. And both are triumphant!<br /><br />This series is everything a true fan of romance could want or need, and this final installment was absolute PERFECTION in every single way!! The heat and chemistry between Colton and Rylee were, as usual, blistering! The depth of character and feeling only continued to build from the second book, Fueled, and, oh, the emotional voyage Rylee and Colton--especially Colton--took me on!!<br /><br /><br />"Fuck being broken or bent, I'm a motherfucking scrapyard of parts right now." <br /><br /><br /><br />"Remember, hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn't it good to be alive?"<br /><br /><br /><br />"His eyes lock onto mine and I try to pour everything in myself into our visual conversation. <br />I accept you, I tell him.<br />All of you.<br />The broken parts. <br />The best parts.<br />The ones filled with shame.<br />The cracks where hope eeks through.<br />The little boy cowering in fear and the grown man still suffocating in its shadow.<br />The demons that haunt.<br />Your will to survive.<br />And your spirit that fights.<br />Every single part of you is what I love.<br />What I accept.<br />What I want to help heal."<br /><br /><br />Colton finally fought the ultimate battle this time around. His opponent? Himself, obviously. He fought the demons he knew and those he only came to learn about. As always, at points, he fought his present, as well. Honestly, there were so many moments when I wondered how he could still be standing, how he could still be fighting. Even at his lowest, he defined inner strength. And the love and devotion of an equally strong woman? Standing, sitting, laying...talking, fighting, or making love...these two could conquer anything together!<br /><br />Crashed is truly--sincerely--remarkable and breathtaking!! K Bromberg's gift--her natural writing and storytelling ability, which has been seasoned and honed to a fine point--shines like the brightest star in this final leg of Rylee and Colton's journey! She deftly ties up every plot point, answering all of those questions along the way. She leaves no one behind. Everyone is accounted for. And if the ending doesn't leave you sniffling and joy-filled, you have no heart!<br /><br />I have no hesitation in stating that Crashed will make you smile and laugh with glee. It will make you sigh with a heart full of romance. You may very well blush with the intensity of the physicality between Colton and Rylee...or, more likely, ruin some undergarments! And Crashed will leave you in tears from the sheer pain, anguish, and, ultimately, the raw beauty of emotional growth.<br /><br /><br />10+ Stars!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="820134051479600082" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
