              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14326290013019071198"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391568351i/8412288._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>4.5 "Motherf*cking checkered flag " STARS</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394596992ra/8875683.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Relationships aren’t easy. They’re hard and can be brutal at times…but those are the times you learn the most about yourself. And when they’re right,” I pause, making sure his eyes are steadfast on mine, “they can be like coming home…finding the rest of your soul…” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy Cow! This was the most intense, crazy emotional, and angst ridden book of the s</span>
  <span id="freeText14326290013019071198" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391568351i/8412288._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4.5 "Motherf*cking checkered flag " STARS</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394596992ra/8875683.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Relationships aren’t easy. They’re hard and can be brutal at times…but those are the times you learn the most about yourself. And when they’re right,” I pause, making sure his eyes are steadfast on mine, “they can be like coming home…finding the rest of your soul…” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy Cow! This was the most intense, crazy emotional, and angst ridden book of the series. I felt like I spent 90% of the book crying, bawling or just tearing up. But it was also the book I most enjoyed from the whole series. As soon as I began reading the Prologue, the tears just came pouring out. I connected so deeply with these characters in this book. I felt. Every. Single. Emotion. They were feeling themselves. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>‘Fuck if she’s not everything I need and nothing that I deserve.’ <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book picks up immediately where the last book left off. Which had ended in quite the cliffhanger. I am just SO glad I didn't have to wait to read what happened next or I would have pulled my hair out. So, like I mentioned before that Prologue had me bawling, it was just so freaking scary, heart breaking and amazing all at once. I really loved it despite it being so sad. Then the first chapter came next, and I felt that desperation Rylee was feeling. I was one of those books where I really just FELT everything. I am really impressed with K. Bromberg and how much her writing has improved. I really enjoyed the way in which she wrote this book and was able to captivate me into the story a lot more than she had on the previous two books.<br><br>I really don't want to give much away about what happens in this story. I think you would get a better reading experience not knowing what's going to happen. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395193825i/8963787._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>I squeeze her a little tighter, not wanting to let her go just yet because, fuck, what racer doesn't want to holdon to their checkered flag a little longer?<br>At least I know mine waves only for me.<br>My kryptonite.<br>My alphabet, motherfucking A to Z.<br><i>My fucking Rylee.</i><br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Rylee went through a tough first half of the book, but that doesn't the second half wasn't tough on her either. Something huge happens to her in the second part. I am so happy it didn't cause her to close up. What I really love about Rylee is that she isn't the usual doormat heroine. She is so strong, and fights for what she wants. She pushed Colton's boundaries while staying by his side when he pushed her away. I love how unconditional her love for him was. Any moment they shared together where they were finally moving forward from Colton's demons, made me extremely happy. They had a connection you can really feel and I LOVED that. It was just so sweet and heart warming seeing them interact that way, with their walls obliterated.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I accept you, I tell him. All of you. The broken parts. The bent parts. The ones filled with shame. The cracks where hope seeps through. The little boy cowering in fear and the grown man still suffocating in his shadow. The demons that haunt. Your will to survive. And your spirit that fights. Every single part of you is what I love. What I accept. What I want to help heal.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395193826i/8963788._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>My handsome, arrogant rougue.<br>A little cocky.<br>A lot imperfect.<br>And completely mine.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Colton goes through a really tough time in this book. It was time for him to finally face all of the demons that had haunted him for most of his life. He was stubborn, hurtful, and frustrating. But this was the only way he knew how to cope with how he was feeling. It was really hard for him, but I am proud of him for accomplishing what he did by the end of the book. I LOVED seeing him open up to Rylee in a way he never had before. He was just so awesome and romantic...who knew? And he said he didn't have it in him. Lies!! Because I seriously loved him so much. He may have broken my heart a few times, but he also made me sigh, pant, and swoon like crazy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430293ra/862650.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You were the one thing I never wanted—never, ever expected in my life—an fuck if I can live without you now. You test me and tempt me and make me look at the truth I don’t want to face and are stubborn as hell, but God, baby, I wouldn’t want you any other way. Wouldn’t want us any other way.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, this book was a tear jerking riot of emotions. It was a long journey for both of them to finally heal. I am quite exhausted now that I have finished it, but I am also so freaking happy for them. There was quite a bit of sex in this book, but for the most part it wasn't those filler types of scenes, they meant something to them. It was a way to show the connection between them. Yes, this book contained a lot of sadness, but there was plenty of happy, playful banter times as well. There was also some sweet and cheesy moments--that I would usually not enjoy--but because of all the tears it worked well here. So, it ended up not bothering me, but instead I ended up liking it. I loved every character and the role they played in the story. What really made me happy was the TWO epilogues. One was in Rylee's perspective, and the other in Colton's--but both were not of the same scene. It was beautiful and perfect and warmed my heart. I cried too, but thankfully they were HAPPY tears this time...ha! I loved this last book and I am hoping Becks and Haddie get their own book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I want to be your first, your last, and every fucking thing in between.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14326290013019071198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_863423606" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/863423606" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/863423606?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-reads">march-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer863423606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12318766495007360803"> "Life isn't about how you survive the storm,<br/> but rather how you dance in the rain."<br/><br/>I have been absolutely brought to my knees with the final installment to this highly emotional,sexy, and romantic story. "Crashed" was by far the most intense book of the trilogy, and my absolute favorite. This conclusion to Rylee and Colton's love affair was a journey of extreme highs and lows...in the end though the pain that this couple endured and suffered through, carried them all of the way to the finish li</span>
  <span id="freeText12318766495007360803" style="display:none"> "Life isn't about how you survive the storm,<br /> but rather how you dance in the rain."<br /><br />I have been absolutely brought to my knees with the final installment to this highly emotional,sexy, and romantic story. "Crashed" was by far the most intense book of the trilogy, and my absolute favorite. This conclusion to Rylee and Colton's love affair was a journey of extreme highs and lows...in the end though the pain that this couple endured and suffered through, carried them all of the way to the finish line; which was a thing of beauty when all was said and done. K. Bromberg is an amazing author who delivered a series that most readers will find impossible to forget. Her characters came to life and they will be forever etched into my heart for years to come.<br /><br />This book was heavy duty, and at times I became an emotional wreck. Colton and Rylee are given more than their fair share of angst; but I was amazed at the strength both of them had to pull through and fight for each other. In the beginning of the story Colton is the one that is down, and Rylee is devastated that she may lose him. When I say that she was devastated; that is definitely an understatment. I seriously though that she was going to fall apart and never be able to pick up the pieces ever again. I will say that Rylee gave me a huge surprise when she eventually pulled up her big girl panties and fought hard for Colton in a variety of different ways. Rylee is by far one of the most strongest heroine's I have ever read about, and it was wonderful to see her transformation from the first book all the way to the last. She had her work cut out for her with Colton always trying to put up road blocks when he felt he was getting too emotionally vulnerable. Not only would Colton shut down; but he could be down right cruel, and Rylee never backed down. Becks, who was Colton's closest friend, also played a huge role in trying to keep Rylee and Colton on the right track. He was fundamental in their success, and I hear there will be a book coming out about him and I will be standing in line for that one for sure!<br /><br />Colton was the one that showed the most transformation. He went from being majorly damaged to realizing his extreme love for Rylee. His journey had me close to tears more than once, and it was heartbreaking to hear what this guy had happen to him as a child. I was glued to the pages during most of Colton's journey, and the author did such a good job with writing the scenes I could taste his pain and frustration. I felt like I was living right alongside of Colton and it broke my heart. (I sat in the parking lot at the grocery store for a few hours because I couldn't put the book down!!) I realize I am not giving any details to the story; but it is a trilogy that I wouldn't want to disclose any details to someone who is thinking of reading it. This is a series that I highly recommend, and I promise you won't be disappointed!<br /><br />I will say the scavenger hunt at the end of Crashed was so heartwarming. It was a bittersweet ending to the series and I loved the uniqueness of it! To take us down memory lane through all three books was brilliant.It was a beautiful reminder of what these two had gone through to get them to where they were at this time! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12318766495007360803" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_617739082" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617739082" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617739082?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617739082" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5378554457800416842"><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393816822i/8768196._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Jenny:</b> I have to say, I experienced mixed emotions picking up this final installment in the Driven Trilogy. There was jubilation at the thought of spending more time with Rylee, Colton and the gang, yet sadness in thinking…this is it. This is the final installment in a series that gripped me and held me captive all the way through…from the first page of Driven to the last page of Crashed and we’ve been there from its beginning to its conclusion. It’s always tough saying goodbye to cha</span>
  <span id="freeText5378554457800416842" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Stars </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393816822i/8768196._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jenny:</b> I have to say, I experienced mixed emotions picking up this final installment in the Driven Trilogy. There was jubilation at the thought of spending more time with Rylee, Colton and the gang, yet sadness in thinking…this is it. This is the final installment in a series that gripped me and held me captive all the way through…from the first page of Driven to the last page of Crashed and we’ve been there from its beginning to its conclusion. It’s always tough saying goodbye to characters when they have cemented a place in your heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Help me. Save me. Redeem me.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Crashed picked up right where we were left gasping and peeling our fingers off our Kindles in Fueled. K Bromberg has certainly given us some heart palpitating moments and her cliffhangers are legendary! But we always forgave her because what she achieved through those cliffys was to build up the anticipation for the next book, and luckily for us, she never kept us waiting too long. One thing for certain…she certainly made us want to dive straight in after she left us hanging!<br><br><b>
  <i>“Relationships aren’t easy. They’re hard and can be brutal at times…but those are the times you learn the most about yourself….”</i>
</b><br><br>First up, that prologue. Wow! K Bromberg, you never fail to hook me in with your engrossing prologues and Crashed was no exception. What a way to kick it off! Seriously, I don’t think I moved except to turn the page. It was tragic, heartbreaking, moving and the suspense garnered in those scenes had me riveted and on the edge of my seat.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t be your spark if I can’t feel yours, so don’t you dare burn out on me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Rylee’s pain and heartbreak seeps through the pages of Crashed as you feel the fragile grip she has on her sanity and her heart during some heart stopping moments. Rylee’s strength amazed me and she really digs deep in Crashed. To experience Colton’s fears first hand, his fear of life, his fear of love, his fear of happiness and his fear of facing his past was powerful to say the least and it’s all brought together so poignantly and beautifully in Crashed. K Bromberg really has done her readers proud in this final instalment.<br><br><b>
  <i>“How could I walk away from those eyes and the smile I knew was hiding somewhere beneath the fear and shame”</i>
</b><br><br>There were times in Crashed when I found myself clutching my chest with anticipation and there were times when the pure emotion of some scenes would come crashing down on me. Rylee and Colton’s story is brought to a gripping and moving conclusion that had my heart racing a few times and relishing in the growth between Rylee and Colton. I have to say, the moments between Colton and his father reduced me to a snivelling wreck. This instalment was an emotionally charged, adrenaline filled, steamy and passionate read with the trademark cheekiness, humor and warmth we’ve come to love. Yep! I “race” this series!<br><br><b>Gitte:</b> I’m always filled with trepidation before starting the third and last book in a trilogy I love. The apprehension stemming from falling in love with the characters, living what seems a life-time with them, crying, laughing, swooning and fearing with and over them. However, once I started Crashed I felt like it was only yesterday we were left in that horrible freeze frame moment that tore our hearts out. But not only that, I have to say K. Bromberg is the Queen of Prologues in my opinion, no question about it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>She sucks you into the story again within a few words, and that’s you hooked all over again inhaling every word feeling warm and possessive over Rylee and Carlton. Because truly I do, this couple have cemented their place in the top of my list of all-time favourite couples. I love them with all my heart.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You came from a place of unfathomable pain and yet you…you’re this incredible light who has helped to heal me, has helped to heal my boys.”</i>
</b><br><br>Seriously, how much have we been through with these two, all of it so heart breaking yet so passion-filled and emotional. Nevertheless, there’s so much still for them to resolve within themselves and with others, in order to find their true happiness without living in the shadows of the past and in the shadows of the ones who wronged them.<br><br><b>
  <i>‘…we need to crack. We need to break. Only then can we pick up each other’s pieces and make each other whole again.’</i>
</b><br><br>Oh and then there’s that ‘little’ issue of how we were left at the end of Fueled!! My pulse was racing…..pun totally intended!<br><br>Colton broke me, he reduced me to a crying mess and at times I truly wished I could’ve jumped into the kindle and demanded calm – order and maybe a few hits. Oh and in between the heart-break we had the passionate all-consuming sex on bloody legs who reduced me to a puddle…on a spoon….that…yeah I’m going to stop here!<br><br><b>
  <i>“..I want to be your first, your last, and every fucking thing in between.” – Colton</i>
</b><br><br>Colton went through the ringer in Crashed, but he needed to in order to resolve his emotions, learn who he truly is and realise that what others may have inflicted on you does not determine the man you become. Only you determine that. You chose your destiny when you realise the man you want to be; what prints you want to leave in life. Now that is not an easy feat nor is it something that just happens, it’s bloody hard all things considering, so bless our Rylee.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Why do you love me, Rylee?”</i>
</b><br><br>Rylee truly grew in Crashed and showed Carlton what an amazing man he is, how much he’s loved and how he inspires everything good in those who love him who are loved by him in return. She also went through one hell of a journey in Crashed; so many obstacles, so much pain and heart-ache. Yet she fought like a soldier and stood steadfast when everything around her crumbled. I cried many tears alongside her.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Don’t you know? You’re my motherfucking chequered flag.”</i>
</b><br><br>There were so many scenes of astounding sublime genius where you hold your breath, your heart bleeds and you feel every single word. Scenes where you watch as events play out before you and you marvel at the brilliance of K. Bromberg. I ‘lego’ this series to the moon and back and I ‘race’ Colton and Rylee!<br><br><b>
  <i>“A to the motherfucking Z “</i>
</b>… Kristy!!!! Oh and <b>
  <i>“…you will never be inconsequential.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>J&amp;G:</b> We can’t help but marvel at the growth K Bromberg has shown as an author since we first sampled her writing when we devoured Driven mid last year. Not only that, but she has allowed her characters to grow right along with her.<br><br>Rylee and Colton’s story has been tumultuous, passionate, engrossing, emotional and beautiful, with a heat factor that has been off the charts. It has become one of our favourite series, and one we’ve never hesitated in recommending to our fellow readers.<br><br>In this final installment K Bromberg delivered. She encapsulated the trials and tribulations, the pitfalls and successes, the love and the heartbreak that has been Colton and Rylee’s journey in The Driven Trilogy and we’re so happy to have been there from the start of the race to the chequered flag!<br><br><b>
  <i>‘Fuck if she’s not everything I need and nothing that I deserve.’</i>
</b><br><br>So why not a 5 star you ask. Whilst Crashed delivered on so many counts there were a couple of sub plots we felt stilted the flow of the story for us. We did however find ourselves a little conflicted on these because the eventual conclusions were an integral part of the story and the relationship between Rylee and Colton and what transpired from them did have us clutching our hearts and sobbing.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Remember, hurting is feeling and feeling is living and isn’t it good to be alive?”</i>
</b><br><br>Ohhh that Epilogue…it was pure perfection! Sigh………It’s with a heavy heart that we bid Rylee and Colton farewell. You’ll be missed guys.<br><br><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5378554457800416842" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_606727087" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/606727087" />
    <a title="J" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10343430-j"><img alt="J" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/606727087?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J" href="/user/show/10343430-j">J</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10343430-j?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer606727087" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10541245300870682717"><br/><div>
  <br/>
  <i>
    <a href='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OrdUjBX4o_E/UxPPhrwDV1I/AAAAAAAABes/RSX83DQ3KaY/s1600/Crashed+Collage+.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
      <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393810019i/8767104._SX540_.jpg' height='260' width='640' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
    </a>
  </i>
</div><br/><div>
<br/>A Book, that needs not to be reviewed but to sit in post reading after math and bask in all it's GLORY!<br/><br/>Brilliant, absolutely brilliant….<br/>This series will forever be in my heart. <br/>Cause K.Bromberg….<br/><br/><b><i>You captured my heart, stole it, broke it, healed it, and will forever own a part of it.</i></b>
</div><br/><div>
  <br/>
  <br/>
</div><br/>Have you ever experienced something that you wish you had the power to un-experience just to experience it all over again?<br/>This was one of those times for me. Colton and Rylee's jour</span>
  <span id="freeText10541245300870682717" style="display:none"><br><div>
  <br>
  <i>
    <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OrdUjBX4o_E/UxPPhrwDV1I/AAAAAAAABes/RSX83DQ3KaY/s1600/Crashed+Collage+.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393810019i/8767104._SX540_.jpg" height="260" width="640" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </i>
</div><br><div>
<br>A Book, that needs not to be reviewed but to sit in post reading after math and bask in all it's GLORY!<br><br>Brilliant, absolutely brilliant….<br>This series will forever be in my heart. <br>Cause K.Bromberg….<br><br><b><i>You captured my heart, stole it, broke it, healed it, and will forever own a part of it.</i></b>
</div><br><div>
  <br>
  <br>
</div><br>Have you ever experienced something that you wish you had the power to un-experience just to experience it all over again?<br>This was one of those times for me. Colton and Rylee's journey is one that will honestly stay with me forever. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"What do you mean?" <br>"Are you okay?"he asks again. <br>"You seem kind of broken." </i>
</b><br><br><br><br>K. Bromberg is the master of story telling, it's more than words in a book, its the emotion and the journey, the absolute pull she has on you. She delivers the kind of intensity rarely seen in today's Romantic Genre.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>I've been robbed of every emotion but fear.</i>
</b><br><br><br><br>I'm blown away by her respect to her readers in delivering the ending that Colton and Rylee deserves.<br>And the respect to the power of her words, the power to break you down, tear you apart, then slowly and carefully put you back together.<br>Her dedication to the relationship of Colton and Rylee, is one that very few can master. Reading and experiencing Crashed hurt to read, you physically ache! K. draws so much raw emotion from you, you don't know how you will ever recover. And that's REAL. It's real and devastatingly ugly yet so amazingly beautiful.<br>It's intimate and heartbreaking, and one of the most unbelievable things you will ever read.<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn't it good to be alive?" </i>
</b><br><br><br><br>Hands down there will be no other. She came she wrote and she concurred. <br><br><br>Now the question for all those die hard fans. Can it match the previous books?<br>I guarantee come day after release you will have thousands of readers walking on air saying, <br>I read it, I experienced it, and I still don't believe it! <br><br><br><b>
  <i>And then you Crashed into my life…. </i>
</b><br><br><br><br>Bravo K.Bromberg, the Queen of Prologues, Master of Epilogues, and and ruler of everything in between. From the bottom of my heart you my friend have set the bar so very high, people will have to scale buildings to reach it….. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b><br><br>✦★☆ 10 There will be NO OTHER Stars ☆✦★<br><br>Buy it <br>Read it <br>Love it </b>
</blockquote><br><br><div>

  <b>A definite 6 star book for me...ending this series that became one of my all time favorite series ever...</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"I want to be your mother fucking checkered flag, Rylee. Your pace car to lead you through tough times,your pit stop when you need a break, your start line, your finish line, your goddamn victory lane..</b>

  <span id="freeText11742707286004527540" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>A definite 6 star book for me...ending this series that became one of my all time favorite series ever...</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"I want to be your mother fucking checkered flag, Rylee. Your pace car to lead you through tough times,your pit stop when you need a break, your start line, your finish line, your goddamn victory lane..</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394405256i/8849206.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So f'king amazing.. I couldn't turn the pages fast enough.. I was hooked, enthralled, gutted and captivated by this amazing story.. all 3 books were beyond what I could have imagined. I waited until this last book in the series was out so I could enjoy them all together and I'm so glad I did. I would have died a bit having to wait between each story. Absofreaking died.. <br><br>So sad it's over.....but what a beautiful epilogue.. <br><br>Thank you K., for such and amazing story..you've found a fan for life... xoxoxoxoxo<br><br><br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1810035228" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15450754064702219053">Get it here: <br/><a href='https://amzn.to/2R8VEWX' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='https://amzn.to/2QgyEUK' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1538182047ra/26369058.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am calling out all of my "friends" who have read these books and saying how dare you not tie me down and force me to read this trilogy before now. I honestly don't know why I waited so long to start the books but once I did I literally could not put them down. After I picked up <i>Driven</i> I stayed up all night reading until the very end of <i>Crashed</i>. I was just completely hooked and Colton and Rylee had me begging for more. <br/><br/>Their story was emotional and sweet but wi</span>
  <span id="freeText15450754064702219053" style="display:none">Get it here: <br><a href="https://amzn.to/2R8VEWX" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="https://amzn.to/2QgyEUK" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1538182047ra/26369058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am calling out all of my "friends" who have read these books and saying how dare you not tie me down and force me to read this trilogy before now. I honestly don't know why I waited so long to start the books but once I did I literally could not put them down. After I picked up <i>Driven</i> I stayed up all night reading until the very end of <i>Crashed</i>. I was just completely hooked and Colton and Rylee had me begging for more. <br><br>Their story was emotional and sweet but with that bad boy hotness added to it to bring all the sexiness. There was drama thrown in but it was so well done that it was never too much that it overwhelmed the romance part of the book. Instead I really enjoyed it and loved how K. Bromberg had me on the edge of my seat practically dying to get all of the answers about these characters. <br><br>I honestly don't even know what to say to describe how much I enjoyed this reading experience so I'll just leave this review at saying that if you haven't picked these books up yet you are majorly missing out. Colton and Rylee are definitely a couple you need to read about.</span>

<div id="review_616530674" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/616530674" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/616530674?book_show_action=true">May 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616530674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5143009563013002213"><b>"4 A to the Motherfucking Z Stars"</b><br/><br/>We were left with a bit of a huge cliffy at the end of "Driven", and it was torture waiting all these long months for "Crashed".<br/>We had to wait to find out the fate of Colton.<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/crash_zps7b9f026f.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840940.gif' alt=' photo crash_zps7b9f026f.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/Supernatural-Gif-supernatural-33019501-500-279_zps78b852b1.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840941.gif' alt=' photo Supernatural-Gif-supernatural-33019501-500-279_zps78b852b1.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Colton is rushed to the hospital after being critically injured in that Crash at the end of book 2.<br/>Rylee is hanging on by a thread.<br/>Her whole life has been flipped on its axis.<br/>Just when she and Colton were taking their relationship to the next </span>
  <span id="freeText5143009563013002213" style="display:none"><b>"4 A to the Motherfucking Z Stars"</b><br><br>We were left with a bit of a huge cliffy at the end of "Driven", and it was torture waiting all these long months for "Crashed".<br>We had to wait to find out the fate of Colton.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/crash_zps7b9f026f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840940.gif" alt=" photo crash_zps7b9f026f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/Supernatural-Gif-supernatural-33019501-500-279_zps78b852b1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840941.gif" alt=" photo Supernatural-Gif-supernatural-33019501-500-279_zps78b852b1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Colton is rushed to the hospital after being critically injured in that Crash at the end of book 2.<br>Rylee is hanging on by a thread.<br>Her whole life has been flipped on its axis.<br>Just when she and Colton were taking their relationship to the next level, tragedy strikes<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zpsd6e12fa2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394348693i/8840942._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsd6e12fa2.jpg" height="400" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>It's pretty early on in the book and so you're safe in assuming that Colton is going to pull through.<br>The only issue is he has a bit of memory loss but he still remembers Rylee and their time together.<br>He just doesn't remember something important he said to her just before he got into his car at the beginning of the race.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps12f67925.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394348693i/8840943._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps12f67925.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This story was very well written and I love how the author creates secondary characters who are so memorable and bring some really touching moments to the story.<br>I loved the interactions between Colton and his father.<br>Some scenes had me in tears.<br><br><br>Colton is finally getting his act together in this one.<br>He tries his bullshit with pushing Rylee away, but she's not having any of it.<br>I loved Ryles for her strength and tenacity.<br>She knows in her heart that this man loves her, even if he can't say the words, and this time she's willing to stand up and fight for their love.<br><br><br>Of course the sex is off the charts HOT again.<br>Was there ever any doubt?<br>These two have such combustible chemistry and you will be fanning yourself tons while reading this book.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mqcwkr6cN51rz2cbjo1_500_zps50248e1c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840944.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mqcwkr6cN51rz2cbjo1_500_zps50248e1c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Everything can't be all rainbows and unicorns in this story.<br>If you've read the first two books, you will know K. Bromberg is very good at dishing out the "ANGST".<br>And there was a TREMENDOUS amount of angst in this last installment.<br>I found myself needing to take a breather quite often from the whiplash I was getting from it.<br>Every time it seemed Colton and Rylee made it through one fucked up situation, another one was right around the corner waiting to stir shit up again.<br><br>Tawny, was a straight up bitch and I was glad how things ended up where she's concerned.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/814235_zpsef835340.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394348693ra/8840945.gif" alt=" photo 814235_zpsef835340.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Even though I really did love this one.<br>I couldn't give it a five.<br>My god this was one long book.<br>I think it should have been shortened just a little bit.<br><br><br><br>There was waaaaaaay too much angst.<br>I love angst.<br>I really do!!<br>It was just all too much.<br>I was feeling so bad for these two. <br>They never could catch a break.<br><br><br>Colton is the one who changes the most in this last installment.<br>I loved seeing his walls come down.<br>He finally realizes that Rylee is the love of his life and his savior.<br><br>Everyone who has fallen in love with this series since "Driven", will absolutely love this conclusion.<br>The Epilogues, yes there are two epilogues, were perfect!<br><br><br><br><b>Call me a pussy, but I swear to God she's the only air my body can breathe. Fuck if she's not everything I need and nothing that I deserve.</b><br><br><br><br><b>Her eyes finally find and lock onto mine. All I see is my future, my salvation, my singular chance at redemption.</b><br><br><br><br><b>"Well, if you think I fuck like I drive, you should see me drop the hammer and</b> <i>
  <b>race</b>
</i> <b>you to the finish line."</b><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I'm the only one that's allowed to drive you to the motherfucking checkered flag."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><b>Those violet eyes of hers--the only ones that have ever been able to see straight into my soul and see everything I've hidden--blink back tears and try to process what I've been telling her I've never wanted, I now want with her.<br>Tomorrows.<br>Possibilities.<br>A fucking future.<br>The ultimate motherfucking checkered flag.</b></span>

<div id="review_699497804" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/699497804" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/699497804?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer699497804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10137035647047349062"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393816822i/8768196._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b> J&G: 4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Jenny:</b> I have to say, I experienced mixed emotions picking up this final instalment in the Driven Trilogy. There was jubilation at the thought of spending more time with Rylee, Colton and the gang, yet sadness in thinking…this is it. This is the final instalment in a series that gripped me and held me captive all the way through…from the first page of Driven to the last page of Crashed and we’ve been there from its beginning to its conclusion. It’s always tough saying goodbye to </span>
  <span id="freeText10137035647047349062" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393816822i/8768196._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> J&amp;G: 4.5 Stars<br><br>Jenny:</b> I have to say, I experienced mixed emotions picking up this final instalment in the Driven Trilogy. There was jubilation at the thought of spending more time with Rylee, Colton and the gang, yet sadness in thinking…this is it. This is the final instalment in a series that gripped me and held me captive all the way through…from the first page of Driven to the last page of Crashed and we’ve been there from its beginning to its conclusion. It’s always tough saying goodbye to characters when they have cemented a place in your heart.<br><br><b>Help me. Save me. Redeem me.</b><br><br>Crashed picked up right where we were left gasping and peeling our fingers off our Kindles in Fueled. K Bromberg has certainly given us some heart palpitating moments and her cliffhangers are legendary! But we always forgave her because what she achieved through those cliffys was to build up the anticipation for the next book, and luckily for us, she never kept us waiting too long. One thing for certain…she certainly made us want to dive straight in after she left us hanging!<br><br><b>
  <i>“Relationships aren’t easy. They’re hard and can be brutal at times…but those are the times you learn the most about yourself….”</i>
</b><br><br>First up, that prologue. Wow! K Bromberg, you never fail to hook me in with your engrossing prologues and Crashed was no exception. What a way to kick it off! Seriously, I don’t think I moved except to turn the page. It was tragic, heartbreaking, moving and the suspense garnered in those scenes had me riveted and on the edge of my seat.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t be your spark if I can’t feel yours, so don’t you dare burn out on me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Rylee’s pain and heartbreak seeps through the pages of Crashed as you feel the fragile grip she has on her sanity and her heart during some heart stopping moments. Rylee’s strength amazed me and she really digs deep in Crashed. To experience Colton’s fears first hand, his fear of life, his fear of love, his fear of happiness and his fear of facing his past was powerful to say the least and it’s all brought together so poignantly and beautifully in Crashed. K Bromberg really has done her readers proud in this final instalment.<br><br><b>
  <i>“How could I walk away from those eyes and the smile I knew was hiding somewhere beneath the fear and shame”</i>
</b><br><br>There were times in Crashed when I found myself clutching my chest with anticipation and there were times when the pure emotion of some scenes would come crashing down on me. Rylee and Colton’s story is brought to a gripping and moving conclusion that had my heart racing a few times and relishing in the growth between Rylee and Colton. I have to say, the moments between Colton and his father reduced me to a snivelling wreck. This instalment was an emotionally charged, adrenaline filled, steamy and passionate read with the trademark cheekiness, humor and warmth we’ve come to love. Yep! I “race” this series!<br><br><b>Gitte:</b> I’m always filled with trepidation before starting the third and last book in a trilogy I love. The apprehension stemming from falling in love with the characters, living what seems a life-time with them, crying, laughing, swooning and fearing with and over them. However, once I started Crashed I felt like it was only yesterday we were left in that horrible freeze frame moment that tore our hearts out. But not only that, I have to say K. Bromberg is the Queen of Prologues in my opinion, no question about it.<br><br><b>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</b><br><br>She sucks you into the story again within a few words, and that’s you hooked all over again inhaling every word feeling warm and possessive over Rylee and Carlton. Because truly I do, this couple have cemented their place in the top of my list of all-time favourite couples. I love them with all my heart.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You came from a place of unfathomable pain and yet you…you’re this incredible light who has helped to heal me, has helped to heal my boys.”</i>
</b><br><br>Seriously, how much have we been through with these two, all of it so heart breaking yet so passion-filled and emotional. Nevertheless, there’s so much still for them to resolve within themselves and with others, in order to find their true happiness without living in the shadows of the past and in the shadows of the ones who wronged them.<br><br><b>
  <i>‘…we need to crack. We need to break. Only then can we pick up each other’s pieces and make each other whole again.’</i>
</b><br><br>Oh and then there’s that ‘little’ issue of how we were left at the end of Fueled!! My pulse was racing…..pun totally intended!<br><br>Colton broke me, he reduced me to a crying mess and at times I truly wished I could’ve jumped into the kindle and demanded calm – order and maybe a few hits. Oh and in between the heart-break we had the passionate all-consuming sex on bloody legs who reduced me to a puddle…on a spoon….that…yeah I’m going to stop here!<br><br><b>
  <i>“..I want to be your first, your last, and every fucking thing in between.” – Colton</i>
</b><br><br>Colton went through the ringer in Crashed, but he needed to in order to resolve his emotions, learn who he truly is and realise that what others may have inflicted on you does not determine the man you become. Only you determine that. You chose your destiny when you realise the man you want to be; what prints you want to leave in life. Now that is not an easy feat nor is it something that just happens, it’s bloody hard all things considering, so bless our Rylee.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Why do you love me, Rylee?”</i>
</b><br><br>Rylee truly grew in Crashed and showed Carlton what an amazing man he is, how much he’s loved and how he inspires everything good in those who love him who are loved by him in return. She also went through one hell of a journey in Crashed; so many obstacles, so much pain and heart-ache. Yet she fought like a soldier and stood steadfast when everything around her crumbled. I cried many tears alongside her.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Don’t you know? You’re my motherfucking chequered flag.”</i>
</b><br><br>There were so many scenes of astounding sublime genius where you hold your breath, your heart bleeds and you feel every single word. Scenes where you watch as events play out before you and you marvel at the brilliance of K. Bromberg. I ‘lego’ this series to the moon and back and I ‘race’ Colton and Rylee!<br><br><b><i>“A to the motherfucking Z “… Kristy!!!! Oh and “…you will never be inconsequential.”</i><br><br>J&amp;G:</b> We can’t help but marvel at the growth K Bromberg has shown as an author since we first sampled her writing when we devoured Driven mid last year. Not only that, but she has allowed her characters to grow right along with her.<br><br>Rylee and Colton’s story has been tumultuous, passionate, engrossing, emotional and beautiful, with a heat factor that has been off the charts. It has become one of our favourite series, and one we’ve never hesitated in recommending to our fellow readers.<br><br>In this final instalment K Bromberg delivered. She encapsulated the trials and tribulations, the pitfalls and successes, the love and the heartbreak that has been Colton and Rylee’s journey in The Driven Trilogy and we’re so happy to have been there from the start of the race to the chequered flag!<br><br><b>
  <i>‘Fuck if she’s not everything I need and nothing that I deserve.’</i>
</b><br><br>So why not a 5 star you ask. Whilst Crashed delivered on so many counts there were a couple of sub plots we felt stilted the flow of the story for us. We did however find ourselves a little conflicted on these because the eventual conclusions were an integral part of the story and the relationship between Rylee and Colton and what transpired from them did have us clutching our hearts and sobbing.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Remember, hurting is feeling and feeling is living and isn’t it good to be alive?”</i>
</b><br><br>Ohhh that Epilogue….it was pure perfection! Sigh……….It’s with a heavy heart that we bid Rylee and Colton farewell. You’ll be missed guys.<br><br><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10137035647047349062" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<div id="review_2079057834" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2079057834" />
    <a title="Hanne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne"><img alt="Hanne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456934758p2/21725822.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2079057834?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hanne" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne">Hanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/30166123-crashed">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21725822-hanne?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21725822-hanne?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21725822-hanne?shelf=coyer_summer2017">coyer_summer2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2079057834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16094261470179456774">I was so glad that I already owned this book after that cliffhanger of Fueled. I was still shocked about what happened and I needed to know what happened next, so I started this book immediately. I was hooked from the start and I didn’t want to put this book down. Crashed was amazing!<br/><br/>There were many beautiful, romantic, touching and hot moments in this book. My favorite moment and the one I still remember clearly after weeks of being finished, is Colton’s last date. It was so swoony, adorable, b</span>
  <span id="freeText16094261470179456774" style="display:none">I was so glad that I already owned this book after that cliffhanger of Fueled. I was still shocked about what happened and I needed to know what happened next, so I started this book immediately. I was hooked from the start and I didn’t want to put this book down. Crashed was amazing!<br /><br />There were many beautiful, romantic, touching and hot moments in this book. My favorite moment and the one I still remember clearly after weeks of being finished, is Colton’s last date. It was so swoony, adorable, beautiful and absolutely perfect. <br /><br />Rylee and Colton are incredible characters. Rylee is sweet, patient, caring, selfless and loving. She’s the perfect woman for Colton. Colton changes a lot, but he’s better now. Rylee makes him think about things he never thought about before. Racing is no longer the only thing that matters in Colton’s life. He would do anything for Rylee. He loves her so much, just like Rylee loves him so much.<br /><br />I absolutely love Rylee and Colton together! They are made for each other. Their relationship wasn’t always easy in the past and their love will even be tested in this book, but both of them fight for their love. Everything was worth it in the end. Their love is strong, beautiful, perfect and solid.<br /><br />Rylee and Colton’s love story was one I’ve been wanting to read for years. I was determined to read it this year and I’m so happy that I did. I’m of course kicking myself for not reading it sooner, but better late than never, right? Each book was better than the previous one. Crashed is my favorite book and deserves more than 5 stars. Crashed has a beautiful epilogue that also was the perfect ending of Rylee and Colton’s love story. I won’t mind rereading this love story at all.<br /><br />This series has some amazing secondary characters. I can’t help but feel sad for the little boys. Rylee is close with all of them and she would do anything for them. Colton is also amazing with those boys. My favorite secondary character would be Becks. I already love him and I can’t wait to read his story (Slow Burn). I love his friendship with Colton. Becks knows him through and through and he would always have his back.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16094261470179456774" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer287178984420882769"><i> Re-read september 2016 </i><br/><b> <i> <blockquote> I’m driven by fear…<br/>… Fueled with desperation …<br/>… Crashing into the unknown. </blockquote></i></b>  <br/>Crashed starts exactly where Fueled left off. Colton is fighting for his life and Rylee is there by his side fighting and waiting for him to come back to her. <br/><b> <i> <blockquote>I accept you.<br/>All of you. <br/>The broken parts. <br/>The bent parts.<br/>The ones filled with shame. <br/>The cracks where hope seeps through. <br/>The little boy cowering in fear and the grown man still suffocating in his shadow. <br/>The demons that haunt. <br/>Your w</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText287178984420882769" style="display:none"><i> Re-read september 2016 </i><br /><b> <i> <blockquote> I’m driven by fear…<br />… Fueled with desperation …<br />… Crashing into the unknown. </blockquote></i></b>  <br />Crashed starts exactly where Fueled left off. Colton is fighting for his life and Rylee is there by his side fighting and waiting for him to come back to her. <br /><b> <i> <blockquote>I accept you.<br />All of you. <br />The broken parts. <br />The bent parts.<br />The ones filled with shame. <br />The cracks where hope seeps through. <br />The little boy cowering in fear and the grown man still suffocating in his shadow. <br />The demons that haunt. <br />Your will to survive. <br />And your spirit that fights. <br />Every single part of you is what I love. <br />What I accept. <br />What I want to help heal. </blockquote></i></b>  <br />As emotional, moving, exciting, and at times playful and funny as the other books are, Crashed reaches new heights. A touching love story about two very damaged people who are finally able to heal themselves through their love.<br /><b> <i> <blockquote> Remember, hurting is feeling and feeling is living, and isn’t it good to be alive? </blockquote></i></b>  <br /> K. Bromberg is an amazing and talented writer and completely blew me away. All those little perfect pieces put together. Just perfect!<br />I loved everything about this book from start to finish it was an overall fantastic read.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/JHUdNsqFjceBTqEQUV9fdBZGovUz40rvowK5P/qo9OKu66jRkE5rInQKvUoyfwUmrhH5GiIiANXjSVIBl3O6w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nIUKc3A7tY295ZJbTrdrWOLxCnJTihYSMbx3mggVvCbqr3Ck7VCaFiowgionO+oxqBBXHe/NEzrYvVg28aLRHg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer4207078526255847495"><b><i>New York Times</i> Bestselling author K. Bromberg writes contemporary novels that contain a mixture of sweet, emotional, a whole lot of sexy, and a little bit of real. She likes to write strong heroines, and damaged heroes who we love to hate but can’t help to love.<br/><br/>A mom of three, she plots her novels in between school runs and soccer practices, more often than not with her laptop in tow.<br/><br/>Since publish</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4207078526255847495" style="display:none"><b><i>New York Times</i> Bestselling author K. Bromberg writes contemporary novels that contain a mixture of sweet, emotional, a whole lot of sexy, and a little bit of real. She likes to write strong heroines, and damaged heroes who we love to hate but can’t help to love.<br /><br />A mom of three, she plots her novels in between school runs and soccer practices, more often than not with her laptop in tow.<br /><br />Since publishing her first book on a whim in 2013, Kristy has sold over one and a half million copies of her books across sixteen different countries and has landed on the New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal Bestsellers lists over thirty times. Her Driven trilogy (Driven, Fueled, and Crashed) is currently being adapted for film by Passionflix with the first movie, Driven, releasing August 10th.<br /><br />With her imagination always in overdrive, she is currently scheming, plotting, and swooning over her latest hero. You can find out more about him or chat with Kristy on any of her social media accounts. The easiest way to stay up to date on new releases and upcoming novels is to sign up for her newsletter (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/254MWtI">http://bit.ly/254MWtI</a>) or text KBromberg to 77948 to receive text alerts when a new book releases.<br /><br /><br /><br /></b><br /><br /><br /><b>Social Media Links:</b><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://facebook.com/AuthorKBromberg">https://facebook.com/AuthorKBromberg</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/KBrombergWrites/">http://pinterest.com/KBrombergWrites/</a><br />Instagram: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://instagram.com/kbromberg13/">https://instagram.com/kbromberg13/</a><br />twitter: @KBrombergDriven<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.KBromberg.com">www.KBromberg.com</a> <br /><br /><b>Completed Titles:</b><br />Series:<br /><i> The Driven Series</i><br />Driven<br />Fueled<br />Crashed<br />Raced<br />Aced<br /><br /><i>The Player Duet </i><br />The Player<br />The Catch<br /><br />Standalones<br />UnRaveled<br />Slow Burn<br />Sweet Ache<br />Hard Beat<br />Down Shift<br />Sweet Cheeks<br />Sweet Rivalry (1,001 Dark Nights Series)<br /><br />Everyday Heroes Standalones<br />Cuffed <br />Combust<br />Cockpit - Late Spring 2018</span>
